Innopolis news 30.03.2020 22:20:18
Dear residents, here is a summary of new rules regarding the new self-isolation regime in the Republic of Tatarstan:

üìå Starting March, 30 you have to self-isolate. You are allowed to leave home only in case of emergency (urgent medical help, go to work, go to the nearest grocery store for basic necessities, walk pets at a distance of not more than 100 m from the house, take out garbage).

üìå Keep a distance of at least 1.5 meters on the street and in public places.

üìå March, 31 (tomorrow) we have to reduce the number of buses from Innopolis to Kazan and back as much as possible. Starting April, 1 the buses will be canceled. An updated schedule is here @HelpBot.

üìå Police and Rospotrebnadzor will monitor residents to ensure isolation orders were followed. Be informed there are fines for the violation of the regime.

üìå It is not recommended to leave the territory of the Republic of Tatarstan.

Please follow all the instructions. Everyone's contribution in coping with this difficult situation is extremely important. Take care of yourselves!
